# Track Spline Builder: reflected C++ API


This page documents the supported reflected API that is intended for vehicle setup, Blueprint access, and C++ integration. Names and macro specifiers match the public headers. Internal, legacy-only, deprecated, and experimental members are intentionally omitted.

<div class="api-reference-summary"><span>6 types</span><span>281 UPROPERTY</span><span>18 UFUNCTION</span></div>

## Core components and configuration types

Expand a type to inspect its public properties and functions.

<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>UTrackPhysicsSolverComponent</code><small>177 UPROPERTY · 9 UFUNCTION</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>Public reflected class used by the supported API.</p>
<div><code>UCLASS(ClassGroup = (Vehicles), meta = (BlueprintSpawnableComponent))</code><span>Header: <code>TrackSplineBuilder/Public/TrackPhysicsSolverComponent.h</code></span></div>
</div>

Manual edits remain authoritative.</p><div class="api-member-card__facts"><span><b>Type:</b> <code>ETrackSidePreset</code></span><span><b>Category:</b> Setup|Source</span><span><b>Default:</b> <code>ETrackSidePreset::Auto</code></span><span>Editable · Blueprint</span></div><div class="api-member-card__chips"><code class="api-chip">EditAnywhere</code><code class="api-chip">BlueprintReadWrite</code><code class="api-chip">Category = &quot;Setup|Source&quot;</code><code class="api-chip">meta=(…)</code></div><details class="api-signature"><summary>C++ declaration</summary><pre><code>ETrackSidePreset SidePreset = ETrackSidePreset::Auto;</code></pre></details></div></article>

It also scales the physical-chain slack and extra-sag limits, so large changes affect both the generated target and physical response.</p><div class="api-member-card__facts"><span><b>Type:</b> <code>float</code></span><span><b>Category:</b> Setup|Shape</span><span><b>Default:</b> <code>0.08f</code></span><span>Editable · Blueprint</span></div><div class="api-member-card__chips"><code class="api-chip">EditAnywhere</code><code class="api-chip">BlueprintReadWrite</code><code class="api-chip">Category = &quot;Setup|Shape&quot;</code><code class="api-chip">meta=(…)</code></div><details class="api-signature"><summary>C++ declaration</summary><pre><code>float SuspendedSagRatio = 0.08f;</code></pre></details></div></article>

</details>

## Reflection macro guide

<div class="api-macro-grid">
<article><code>UCLASS</code><p>Registers a UObject-derived class with Unreal reflection. Class metadata controls how the component appears in the editor.</p></article>
<article><code>USTRUCT</code><p>Registers a reflected value type. BlueprintType makes the struct usable as a Blueprint pin and variable type.</p></article>
<article><code>UPROPERTY</code><p>Registers a field for serialization, editor exposure, garbage collection, replication, or Blueprint access according to its specifiers.</p></article>
<article><code>UFUNCTION</code><p>Registers a callable or query function. BlueprintCallable, BlueprintPure, and CallInEditor define where it is exposed.</p></article>
<article><code>GENERATED_BODY</code><p>Injects the code generated by Unreal Header Tool. It must remain inside every reflected class or struct.</p></article>
<article><code>EditAnywhere / VisibleAnywhere</code><p>Controls whether a property is editable or only visible in Details.</p></article>
<article><code>BlueprintReadWrite / BlueprintReadOnly</code><p>Controls whether Blueprint graphs can write the property or only read it.</p></article>
<article><code>Category / meta</code><p>Organizes the editor UI and supplies display names, tooltips, conditions, units, clamps, and advanced-display rules.</p></article>
</div>
